# Product Management

**Industry ID:** `product-management` | **Prefix:** `PROD` | **Target:** 350 bullets

---

### PROD-0001
**Role:** product-manager | **Theme:** roadmap-planning | **Seniority:** mid | **Verb Context:** projects
**Keywords:** product roadmap, OKRs, stakeholder alignment, prioritization, product strategy

**Scope:** a 12-month product roadmap for a {dau}K DAU consumer app across {teams} engineering teams, prioritizing {features} features against {okrs} OKRs through structured discovery
**Result:** delivering {delivered} of {planned} quarterly commitments on time and growing DAU from {dau}K to {dau_after}K within {months} months

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Defined a 12-month roadmap for a {dau}K DAU app across {teams} teams, delivering {delivered} of {planned} quarterly commitments and growing DAU from {dau}K to {dau_after}K in {months} months.
- **B (Result-first):** Grew DAU from {dau}K to {dau_after}K in {months} months and hit {delivered}/{planned} quarterly commitments by owning a 12-month roadmap for a {teams}-team product.
- **C (Impact-led):** Grew DAU from {dau}K to {dau_after}K in {months} months and delivered {delivered}/{planned} commitments on time; defined 12-month product roadmap for a {dau}K-DAU app across {teams} teams.
- **D (Concise):** Owned 12-month roadmap for {teams} teams, DAU from {dau}K to {dau_after}K in {months} months, {delivered}/{planned} quarterly commitments hit.

**Variables:**
  - `{dau}`: 50 to 500, step 50 (integer)
  - `{teams}`: 3 to 8, step 1 (integer)
  - `{features}`: 10 to 40, step 5 (integer)
  - `{okrs}`: 3 to 6, step 1 (integer)
  - `{delivered}`: 8 to 11, step 1 (integer)
  - `{planned}`: 10 to 12, step 1 (integer)
  - `{dau_after}`: 100 to 1000, step 100 (integer)
  - `{months}`: 6 to 12, step 3 (integer)

### PROD-0002
**Role:** product-manager | **Theme:** user-research | **Seniority:** mid | **Verb Context:** operations
**Keywords:** user research, customer interviews, usability testing, Jobs-to-be-Done, product discovery

**Scope:** a product discovery program including {interviews} customer interviews, {surveys} surveys, and {tests} usability tests over {weeks} weeks to validate a new product direction
**Result:** identifying {insights} actionable insights that reshaped {features} features and contributed to a {retention}% improvement in 30-day user retention

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Led a discovery program of {interviews} interviews, {surveys} surveys, and {tests} usability tests, surfacing {insights} insights that reshaped {features} features and improved 30-day retention by {retention}%.
- **B (Result-first):** Improved 30-day retention by {retention}% by leading a discovery program of {interviews} interviews and {tests} usability tests that reshaped {features} key features.
- **C (Impact-led):** Drove {retention}% 30-day retention improvement; ran {interviews} customer interviews, {surveys} surveys, and {tests} usability tests surfacing {insights} insights that reshaped {features} features.
- **D (Concise):** Ran {interviews} interviews, {surveys} surveys, {tests} usability tests, surfaced {insights} insights, reshaped {features} features, 30-day retention up {retention}%.

**Variables:**
  - `{interviews}`: 10 to 50, step 10 (integer)
  - `{surveys}`: 100 to 1000, step 100 (integer)
  - `{tests}`: 5 to 20, step 5 (integer)
  - `{weeks}`: 4 to 12, step 2 (integer)
  - `{insights}`: 10 to 40, step 5 (integer)
  - `{features}`: 3 to 10, step 1 (integer)
  - `{retention}`: 10 to 30, step 5 (percentage)

### PROD-0003
**Role:** product-owner | **Theme:** backlog-management | **Seniority:** mid | **Verb Context:** operations
**Keywords:** backlog refinement, Jira, user stories, sprint planning, backlog grooming

**Scope:** a product backlog of {stories} user stories for a {team}-engineer squad, running bi-weekly grooming sessions and maintaining backlog health across {sprints} sprints
**Result:** increasing sprint commitment accuracy from {before}% to {after}% and reducing carryover stories per sprint from {carry_before} to {carry_after}

**Variations:**
- **A (Standard):** Managed a {stories}-story backlog for a {team}-engineer squad across {sprints} sprints, improving sprint commitment accuracy from {before}% to {after}% and cutting carryover from {carry_before} to {carry_after} stories.
- **B (Result-first):** Improved sprint commitment from {before}% to {after}% and cut carryover from {carry_before} to {carry_after} by managing a {stories}-story backlog for a {team}-person squad across {sprints} sprints.
- **C (Impact-led):** Raised sprint commitment accuracy from {before}% to {after}% and cut carryover from {carry_before} to {carry_after}; managed {stories}-story backlog for {team}-engineer squad over {sprints} sprints.
- **D (Concise):** Managed {stories}-story backlog for {team} engineers over {sprints} sprints, commitment accuracy from {before}% to {after}%, carryover from {carry_before} to {carry_after}.

**Variables:**
  - `{stories}`: 50 to 300, step 50 (integer)
  - `{team}`: 4 to 10, step 1 (integer)
  - `{sprints}`: 6 to 24, step 3 (integer)
  - `{before}`: 60 to 75, step 5 (percentage)
  - `{after}`: 85 to 95, step 5 (percentage)
  - `{carry_before}`: 5 to 15, step 5 (integer)
  - `{carry_after}`: 1 to 3, step 1 (integer)
